SET SQL_MODE="NO_AUTO_VALUE_ON_ZERO";

-- 
-- Database: `conquerserver`
-- 

-- 
-- Table structure for table `accounts`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `accounts` (
  `Username` varchar(16) character set latin1 NOT NULL,
  `Password` varchar(255) character set latin1 NOT NULL,
  `State` tinyint(5) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `EntityID` bigint(18) unsigned NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '1000001',
  `Email` varchar(100) character set latin1 NOT NULL,
  `SecNmbr` bigint(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`EntityID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1000023 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `characters`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `characters` (
  `Name` text NOT NULL,
  `EntityID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '1000001',
  `Account` text NOT NULL,
  `Level` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL default '1',
  `Strength` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Dexterity` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Spirit` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Vitality` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Statpoints` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Money` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '100',
  `ConquerPoints` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `HairStyle` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `Model` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `Class` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `RebornCount` tinyint(150) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Experience` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Hitpoints` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `MaxHitpoints` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `PkPoints` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `Mana` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `MaxMana` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `MapID` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '1002',
  `X` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '438',
  `Y` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '377',
  `GuildID` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `GuildDonation` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `GuildPosition` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `Spouse` varchar(16) NOT NULL default 'None',
  `Avatar` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `Staff` tinyint(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `PrevMap` smallint(5) unsigned NOT NULL default '1002',
  `NobDonation` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `NobRank` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL default '0',
  `NobPosition` int(9) NOT NULL default '-1',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`EntityID`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1000023 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- Table structure for table `expreq`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `expreq` (
  `Level` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Experience` bigint(20) default NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `IP` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `AuthPort` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `GamePort` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `Experience` int(10) unsigned default NULL,
  `WeaponSkill` int(10) unsigned default NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `monsters`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `monsters` (
  `UID` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `Name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `Type` tinyint(4) NOT NULL,
  `Face` smallint(6) NOT NULL,
  `Hitpoints` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `MaxAttack` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `MinAttack` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `Defence` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `Dexterity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `Dodge` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `AttackRange` smallint(6) NOT NULL,
  `ViewRange` smallint(6) NOT NULL,
  `EscapeLife` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `Level` smallint(6) NOT NULL,
  `AttackUser` tinyint(4) NOT NULL,
  `DropMoney` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `DropItemType` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `DropHP` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `DropMP` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `MagicType` tinyint(4) NOT NULL,
  `MagicHitRate` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `MagicDefence` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `AIType` tinyint(4) NOT NULL,
  `Defence2` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `ExtraExp` int(11) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `npc`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `npc` (
  `UID` int(10) unsigned default NULL,
  `X` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `Y` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `MapID` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `Type` smallint(6) default NULL,
  `Facing` int(11) default NULL,
  `Statusflag` int(10) unsigned default NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

--

-- 
-- Table structure for table `portals`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `portals` (
  `CurrentX` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `CurrentY` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `CurrentMapID` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `DestX` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `DestY` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `DestMapID` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `skills`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `skills` (
  `ID` smallint(5) unsigned default NULL,
  `Accuracy` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `BaseDamage` int(10) unsigned default NULL,
  `Ground` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Level` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Mana` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Multitarget` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Offensive` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Range` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Stamina` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Type` tinyint(3) unsigned default NULL,
  `Name` varchar(255) default NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Table structure for table `accountsskills`

  `accountEntityId` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `skillId` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
